
class DatabaseListView extends StatefulWidget {
  const DatabaseListView(
      {Key key, this.context, this.reference, this.itemBuilder})
      : super(key: key);

  final BuildContext context;
  final SpeedReference reference;
  final XenonIndexedWidgetBuilder itemBuilder;

  @override
  _DatabaseListViewState createState() => _DatabaseListViewState();
}

class _DatabaseListViewState extends State<DatabaseListView> {
  @override
  Widget build(BuildContext context) {
    return Center(
        child: loading ? CircularProgressIndicator() : listViewWidget());
  }

  Widget listViewWidget() {
    return ListView.builder(
      itemCount: r['r'].length,
      itemBuilder: (context, index) {
        // return W;
        return widget.itemBuilder(context, r['r'][index]);
      },
    );
  }

  Map<String, dynamic> r;
  bool loading = true;
  XenonBaseDatabase database;

  @override
  void initState() {
    super.initState();

    // making a new database sevrice instance
    database = XenonBaseDatabase.instance;

    void initRef() async {
      r = await widget.reference.get();

      List _l = r['r'];

      List _new = [];

      if (r != null) {
        if (_l != null) {
          _l.forEach((element) {
            _new.add(
              Document.fromMap(element),
            );
          });

          r['r'] = _new;

          loading = false;

          setState(() {});
        }
      }
    }

    initRef();
  }
}

typedef XenonIndexedWidgetBuilder = Widget Function(
    BuildContext context, Document document);
